===============================================================================
  18+ ADULT CONTENT
===============================================================================

Aeternitas is the 18+ edition of this work.

It may include mature themes, strong language, sexual content,
violence, and other material not suitable for minors.

By continuing you confirm that you are at least 18 years old (or the age
of majority where you live) and that viewing such content is lawful for
you. If that is not true, close this program now.

Reputation & patron standing

Autotest Hero â€” a Human adventurer Â· they / them / their

Trade and real conversation move a simple score per merchant. Tiers are plain
labels â€” the fun is in prices and how NPC blurbs feel over time, not grind.

How it moves
  â€¢  Successful talk topics  (+2 base; CHA 15+ +1, CHA 18+ another +1)
  â€¢  Buys and sells here  (+1 each)  â€” repeat visits matter
  â€¢  Gifts (give)  (+3; CHA 14+ +1)  â€” merchant must be present

Effects (when trading here)
  Stranger â†’ better prices as you climb toward Renowned (caps modest so the
  economy cannot break).
